<script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
        jQuery('.search-btn').on('click',function(){
            jQuery('.search-form-wrapper').toggleClass('active');
            jQuery('html').toggleClass('overflow-hidden');
            setTimeout(function(){
                jQuery('.search-form-wrapper input').focus();
            },200);
            
        });  
    });
    function closeSearch(){
        jQuery('html').removeClass('overflow-hidden');
        jQuery('.search-form-wrapper').removeClass('active');
    }
</script>
<script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function() {
        const apiUrl = '/wp-json/mediaset-app-api/v1/programmaOnair';

        function decodeHtmlEntities(text) {
            const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
            textarea.innerHTML = text;
            return textarea.value;
        }
        fetch(apiUrl)
            .then(response => {
                if (!response.ok) {
                    throw new Error(`Network response was not ok: ${response.statusText}`);
                }
                return response.json();
            })
            .then(data => {
                console.log(data);
                if (data && data.onair && data.onair.length > 0) {
                    const onAirProgram = data.onair[0];
                    const titleFM = decodeHtmlEntities(onAirProgram.titoloFM);
                    const imageUrl = onAirProgram.immagineXL;
                    const titleLinkMobile = document.querySelectorAll("#onair-title-link-mobile");
                    if (titleLinkMobile) {
                        titleLinkMobile.forEach(title => {
                            title.textContent = titleFM;
                        });
                    }
                    const titleLinkDesktop = document.querySelectorAll('#onair-title-link-desktop');
                    if (titleLinkDesktop) {
                        titleLinkDesktop.forEach(title => {
                            title.textContent = titleFM;
                        });
                    }
                    const onairImage = document.querySelectorAll("[id='onair-image']");
                    if (onairImage) {
                        onairImage.forEach(title => {
                            title.src = imageUrl;
                            title.alt = titleFM;
                        });
                    }
                } else {}
            })
            .catch(error => {
                const titleLinkMobile = document.querySelectorAll("#onair-title-link-mobile");
                const titleLinkDesktop = document.querySelectorAll('#onair-title-link-desktop');
                const defaultText = 'On Air';

                if (titleLinkMobile) {
                    titleLinkMobile.forEach(title => {
                        title.textContent = defaultText;
                    });
                }
                if (titleLinkDesktop) {
                    titleLinkDesktop.forEach(title => {
                        title.textContent = defaultText;
                    });
                }

                const onairImage = document.querySelectorAll("#onair-image");
                if (onairImage) {
                    onairImage.forEach(title => {
                        title.style.display = 'none';
                    });
                }
            });
    });
</script>

        <script>
            jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
                $('.close-video').on('click', function() {
                    closeAllPlayers();
                });
            });

            function autoPlayList(id) {
                var modal = document.getElementById('playlist-' + id);
                if (!modal) return;

                modal.classList.remove('hidden');
                document.body.classList.add('open-modal');

                var iframe = modal.querySelector('iframe');
                if (!iframe) return;

                var dataSrc = iframe.getAttribute('data-src');
                var currentSrc = iframe.getAttribute('src');

                if (dataSrc && (currentSrc === 'about:blank' || !currentSrc)) {
                    iframe.setAttribute('src', dataSrc);
                    iframe.onload = function() {
                        iframe.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"playVideo","args":""}', '*');
                    };
                } else {
                    iframe.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"playVideo","args":""}', '*');
                }
                document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    if (!document.getElementById('playlist-' + id).contains(e.target)) {
                        if (document.body.classList.contains('open-modal') && !e.target.classList.contains(
                                'playlist_img')) {
                            closeAllPlayers();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            function closeAllPlayers() {
                var iframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe');
                var popups = document.querySelectorAll('.playlist-popup');
                popups.forEach(function(popup) {
                    popup.classList.add('hidden');
                });

                document.body.classList.remove('open-modal');
                iframes.forEach(function(iframe) {
                    if (iframe.contentWindow && (iframe.src.indexOf('youtube') > -1 || iframe.src.indexOf('youtu.be') >
                            -1)) {
                        iframe.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"pauseVideo","args":""}', '*');
                    }
                });
            }
        </script>

function getCookie(name) {
  const match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
  return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[2]) : null;
}

function setCookiePubId(name, value, days) {
  const expires = new Date();
  expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
  document.cookie = name+'='+value+';expires='+expires.toUTCString()+';path=/;SameSite=Lax';
}

(function() {
    let publisherId = getCookie('mds_publisher_id');

    if (!publisherId) {
        publisherId = generateUUID();
        setCookie('mds_publisher_id', publisherId, 365); // 12 mesi
    }   
    window.mdsPublisherId = publisherId;
})();

function getIubendaPurposesString(policyId) {
  const cookieName = "_iub_cs-" + policyId;
  const raw = getCookie(cookieName);
  if (!raw) return null;

  try {
    const data = JSON.parse(raw);
    const purposes = data.purposes || {};

    var result = [];
    for (var id in purposes) {
      if (purposes.hasOwnProperty(id)) {
        result.push(id + '=' + (purposes[id] ? 'yes' : 'no'));
      }
    }

    return result.join(';');
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('Errore parsing cookie:', e);
    return null;
  }
}

  var r = document,
    n = "script",
    a = r.createElement(n),
    o = r.getElementsByTagName(n)[0];
  a.src = window.location.protocol + "//" + e.replace("//", ""), t && a.addEventListener("load", function(e) {
    t(null, e)
  }, !1), o.parentNode.insertBefore(a, o)
}

    console.log(str)
    console.log("*********************************************")

function dispatchLoginEvent(event, payload) {
  const loginEvent = new CustomEvent(event, {detail: {payload}});
  window.dispatchEvent(loginEvent);
} 

function initRtiLogin(){
  window.addEventListener("load", function(){
    const rtiLoginConfSite = rtiLoginConf;

    rtiConf = {
      site: {
        apiKey: rtiLoginConfSite.apiKey
      },
      scope: "radiomediaset",
      //"serviceLayerBaseUrl": "https://api-ott-testcomm-fe.mediaset.net/TESTCOMM/play",
      "loginScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-RegistrationLogin",
      "resetPasswordScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-RegistrationLogin",
      "emailVerifiedScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-RegistrationLogin",
      "afterLoginScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-RegistrationLogin",
      "verificationSentScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-RegistrationLogin",
      "pairingScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-RegistrationLogin",
      "editProfileScreenSetId": "BasicScreenset-ProfileUpdate",
      "editProfileStartScreen": "gigya-profile-update-screen"


    };						
    rtiContext = {
      appName: "web//radio-virginradio/noversion",
      deviceId: utag_data.tealium_visitor_id,
    };	

    async(js_rtilogin = rtiLoginConfSite.urlJs, async function () {
      if (window.RTILab && window.RTILab.idm && window.RTILab.idm.RtiLoginKit) {
        window.RTILab.loginKitInstance = new window.RTILab.idm.RtiLoginKit(rtiConf, rtiContext);
        try {
          const initResult = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.init();	
          var str = JSON.stringify(initResult, null, 4);
          log_('initResult: '+str);
          listen(initResult);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(error)
        }
      }					
    });			    
  }, false);
}
  async function listen(userData) {
    const isUserLogged = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.isUserLogged();

    (isUserLogged && userData.statusCode === 'RL_404') ? handleUserLogged(userData) : handleUserNotLogged(userData);
    log_('user_logged isUserLogged => ' + isUserLogged);

    if (jQuery(".user_name").length) {
      if (!isUserLogged) {
        jQuery(document).on("click", ".user_name", handlerClickShowLogin);
    } else {
        jQuery(document).on("click", ".logout", handlerClickLogoutUser);
        jQuery(document).on("click", ".profile", handlerClickShowEditProfile);
    }
    }

    playlistLike(isUserLogged);
}

function playlistLike(isUserLogged)
{

  if(isUserLogged){
  let array_playlist_dom = [];

if(getCookie('vrg_like_playlist')){
    array_playlist_dom = JSON.parse(getCookie('vrg_like_playlist'));
    for(let k=0; k<array_playlist_dom.length; k++){
      jQuery('#playlistWrap-'+array_playlist_dom[k]+' .like_control').addClass('voted');
    }
}
  } else {
    jQuery('.like_control').removeClass('voted');
  }

}

async function increaseLike(postId,nonce){

  const isUserLogged = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.isUserLogged();
  if(isUserLogged){
    var array_playlist = [];
    if(getCookie('vrg_like_playlist')){
        array_playlist = JSON.parse(getCookie('vrg_like_playlist'));
        if(array_playlist.includes(postId)){
          
            jQuery('#playlistWrap-'+postId+' .like_control').addClass('voted');
            return false;
        }else{
            incrementFieldCall(postId,nonce,array_playlist);
          
        }
    }else{
        incrementFieldCall(postId,nonce,array_playlist);
    }

  } else {
    // Mostra il popup di login di RTILab
    handlerClickShowLogin();
  }

}




async function handlerClickShowLogin() {
    try {
        // L'utente sta tentando di effettuare il login
        log_("handlerClickShowLoginV4");

        // Mostra il popup di login di RTILab
        const userData = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.showLogin(rtiContext);

        // Converte i dati utente in stringa JSON per debug
        var str = JSON.stringify(userData, null, 4);
        log_('userData => ' + str);

        // Controllo se la risposta contiene un errore di autenticazione
        if (!userData.hasOwnProperty('statusCode') || userData.statusCode === 'RL_403') {
            throw new Error('Autentication Failed');
        }

        // Gestione del login riuscito
        handleUserLoginSuccessful(userData);

jQuery(document)
  .off("click", ".logout", handlerClickLogoutUser)
  .on("click", ".logout", handlerClickLogoutUser);

jQuery(document)
  .off("click", ".profile", handlerClickShowEditProfile)
  .on("click", ".profile", handlerClickShowEditProfile);

jQuery(document)
  .off("click", ".user_name", handlerClickShowLogin);

rtimenuInitComplete(userData?.data?.userInfo || userData);


        // Dispatch dell'evento di login riuscito
        dispatchLoginEvent("rtiLogin_v4_user-login-successful", userData);

    } catch (error) {
        // L'utente ha annullato il login o si è verificato un errore
        console.error(error);
    }
}


async function handlerClickShowEditProfile() {
    try {
        log_("SHOW EDIT PROFILE V4");

        // Mostra l'editor del profilo tramite RTILab
        const editProfile = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.showEditProfile(rtiContext);

        console.log("Editor profilo aperto con successo:", editProfile);

        // Dispatch dell'evento di successo
        dispatchLoginEvent("rtiLogin_v4_profile-edit-successful", {});

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(error);
    }
}

async function handlerClickLogoutUser() {
    try {
        log_("LOGOUT V4");

        // Effettua il logout con il sistema RTILab
        const userLogout = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.logoutUser(rtiContext);

        // Esegue le operazioni di logout nel frontend
        handleUserLogoutSuccessful();

        rtimenuInitComplete(null);

        // Dispatch dell'evento di logout
        dispatchLoginEvent("rtiLogin_v4_user-logout-successful", {});	

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(error);
    }
}


function handleUserLogoutSuccessful() {
    user_logged = false;

   // Aggiorna il testo del pulsante login
    jQuery(".user_name").text("Accedi | Registrati");

    // Rimuove la classe "logged" se presente
    var buttonLogged = jQuery(".toolbar.logged");
    if (buttonLogged.length) {
        buttonLogged.removeClass("logged");
    }
    jQuery(".profile,.logout").hide();
    // Aggiunge l'event listener al bottone login
    jQuery(".toolbar:not(.logged) .user_name").off("click").on("click", handlerClickShowLogin);
}


function handleUserLoginSuccessful(payload) {
    user_logged = true;

    // Rimuove il click handler precedente
    jQuery(".toolbar .user_name").off("click", handlerClickShowLogin);

    // Imposta il nome utente
    var t = "";
    if (payload.data && payload.data.userInfo) {
        t = payload.data.userInfo.displayName;
    }

    UID = payload.data.userInfo.uid;

    jQuery(".user_name").text(t);
    jQuery(".toolbar").addClass("logged");
    jQuery(".profile,.logout").show();

}


function handleUserNotLogged() {
    user_logged = false;

    jQuery(".user_name").text("Accedi | Registrati");

    var buttonLogged = jQuery(".toolbar.logged");

    if (buttonLogged.length) {
        buttonLogged.removeClass("logged");
    }
    jQuery(".profile,.logout").hide();

    jQuery(".user_name").off("click").on("click", handlerClickShowLogin);
    rtimenuInitComplete(null);
}

function handleUserLogged(payload) {
    user_logged = true;

    jQuery(".toolbar .user_name").off("click", handlerClickShowLogin);


    var t = "";
    if (payload.data && payload.data.userInfo) {
        t = payload.data.userInfo.displayName;
    } else if (payload.data) {
        t = payload.data.userInfo.displayName;
    }

    log_('user_logged mostro il nome => ' + t);

    UID = payload.data.userInfo.uid;

    jQuery(".user_name").text(t);
    jQuery(".toolbar").addClass("logged");
    jQuery(".profile,.logout").show();

    rtimenuInitComplete(payload.data.userInfo);
}

/* function rtimenuInitComplete() {
  var e = document.createEvent("Event");
  e.initEvent("rtimenuInitComplete", !0, !0), window.dispatchEvent(e);
} */

function rtimenuInitComplete(userData) {
  var e = new CustomEvent("rtimenuInitComplete", { detail: userData });
  window.dispatchEvent(e);
}

//squizzati 105
jQuery('button.btn-casting').on('click', async function () {
  const url = jQuery(this).data('url');
  await cvtosquizz(url);
});

async function cvtosquizz(url) {
  if (!window.rtiCastingPlugin) window.rtiCastingPlugin = {};

  rtiCastingPlugin.log = function (type, ...message) {
    (console[type] || console.log)("rtiCastingPlugin:", ...message);
  };

  rtiCastingPlugin.redirectWithToken = async function (url) {
  rtiCastingPlugin.log("debug", "redirect with token", { url });

  const jwt = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.getJWT({
    fields: "firstName,lastName,emails.verified,birthDay,birthMonth,birthYear",
  });

  rtiCastingPlugin.log("debug", "JWT received", jwt ? jwt.substring(0, 20) + "..." : jwt);

  const form = document.createElement("form");
  form.method = "POST";
  form.action = url;

  const input = document.createElement("input");
  input.type = "hidden";
  input.name = "id_token"; // oppure "jwt" se il backend si aspetta questo nome
  input.value = jwt;

  form.appendChild(input);
  document.body.appendChild(form);

  // opzionale: per vedere il form prima della navigazione
  // setTimeout(() => form.submit(), 200);
  form.submit();
};



  rtiCastingPlugin.join = async function (url) {
    if (!(window.RTILab && window.RTILab.loginKitInstance)) {
      rtiCastingPlugin.log("error", "no RTILab.loginKitInstance defined");
      return;
    }

    // Listener una tantum
    window.addEventListener(
      "rtiLogin_v4_user-login-successful",
      () => rtiCastingPlugin.redirectWithToken(url),
      { once: true }
    );

    try {
      const isUserLogged = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.isUserLogged();

      if (isUserLogged) {
        rtiCastingPlugin.log("debug", "logged");
        await rtiCastingPlugin.redirectWithToken(url);
      } else {
        rtiCastingPlugin.log("debug", "userNotLogged");
        handlerClickShowLogin(); // deve esistere
      }
    } catch (e) {
      rtiCastingPlugin.log("error", "login check failed", e);
      handlerClickShowLogin();
    }
  };

  // Eseguo davvero il join
  await rtiCastingPlugin.join(url);
}

function mdsbdLayerPush(event, data) {
    window.mdsbdLayer = window.mdsbdLayer || [];
    window.mdsbdLayer.push({
        event: event,
        page_data: data
    });
}

mdsbdLayerPush("page_view", pageData);


//push su smart pixel
window.wtSmartPush = async function (consentString, page_num = '',customCategory = {},CustomName = {},customParameters = {}) {

    const isUserLogged = await window.RTILab.loginKitInstance.isUserLogged();
    const logged = isUserLogged ? 'yes' : 'no';

    window.mdsPageViewSent = false;

    window.wtSmart = window.wtSmart || [];
    window.wtSmart.push(function (wtSmart) {

        wtSmart.init.set({
            trackId: '112686412066259',
            trackDomain: 't.radiomediaset.it',
            domain: '',
            cookie: '1'
        });

        var wtkValue = wtSmart.utils.parameter('wtk', document.location.href);
        if (wtkValue) {
            wtkValue = "wtk%3D" + wtkValue;
            wtSmart.campaign.data.set({
                id: wtkValue,
                parameter: {}
            });
        }

        wtSmart.session.parameter.add({
            2: window.mdsPublisherId,
            3: logged
        });

        if (isUserLogged) {
          console.log('User is logged in, setting customer data'+ user.uid);
            wtSmart.customer.data.set({
                id: "rm-" + user.uid
            });
        }

      const pageName = CustomName.name ? CustomName.name : "radiomediaset-virginradio-homepage-/";

        wtSmart.page.data.add({
            name: pageName,
            parameter: {
                1: "virginradio-web",
                2: getCleanURL(),
                3: "homepage",
                6: page_num,
                7: "web",
                8: "web//virginradio-web/6.8.3",
                9: consentString
            },
            category: {
                1: "radiomediaset",
                2: "virginradio",
                3: "homepage",
                4: "",
                5: "/",
                6: "homepage",
                7: "",
                9: "",
                10: "radiomediaset"
            }
        });

        if (Object.keys(customCategory).length) {
        wtSmart.page.category.add(customCategory);
    }

        if (Object.keys(customParameters).length) {
        wtSmart.page.parameter.add(customParameters);   
    }


        console.log('page data:', wtSmart.page.data.get());
console.log('page type:', "page");
console.log('single or archive:', "other");

        wtSmart.track(true);

        window._wtSmartInitialized = true;
        window.mdsPageViewSent = true;
    });
};

//push per gallery
    var postId = "/";

    function getCurrentSlideInfo() {
        var slides = jQuery('#postgallery .swiper-slide');
        var total = slides.length;
        var currentIndex = 0;

        slides.each(function(index) {
            if (jQuery(this).hasClass('swiper-slide-active')) {
                currentIndex = jQuery(this).data('swiper-slide-index') + 1; // 1-based index
            }
        });

        return { currentIndex: currentIndex, total: total };
    }

    function pushSlideInfo() {
        var info = getCurrentSlideInfo();
        var output = "virginradio" + ':'+postId + '.' + info.currentIndex + '.' + info.total;
        console.log('Push:', output);

        pageData.page_num = output;
        // Push to mdsbdLayer
        mdsbdLayerPush("page_view", pageData);
        // Push to wtSmart
        wtSmartPush(consentString,output,{},{},{});
    }

    jQuery('#postgallery .swiper-button-next, #postgallery .swiper-button-prev').on('click', function() {
        // Delay per aspettare che la slide si aggiorni
        setTimeout(pushSlideInfo, 100);
    });

        pageData.title = title;
        //var output = "virginradio" + ':' + postId + '.' + playlistIndex + '.' + videoIndex + '.' + totalVideos;
        // Push to mdsbdLayer
        mdsbdLayerPush("page_view", pageData);
        // Push to wtSmart
       // wtSmartPush(consentString,output);
    }

    jQuery('[id^="playlistWrap-"]').on('click', function() {
        var data = jQuery(this);
        setTimeout(function() {
        pushPlaylistInfo(data);
